name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

info:Stayed in June 2024
info:Business travelers
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 5, 2024
msg:Thanks to the platform and the hotel for upgrading the room type.

Room: Very large and clean. The 2-meter bed is very comfortable. In addition to the small sofa, there are also desks and chairs, which is a plus. All facilities are very complete.

Bathroom: The division is very clear. The shower room and toilet are divided into different areas. There are two wash basins on the washbasin, which is convenient for the whole family. There is also a bathtub. Even the ladies' dressing area and dressing mirror are arranged, which is really considerate. The wardrobe door is double-opened on both sides of the corridor and the bathroom. This design space utilization is very appropriate and thoughtful, and it is also very novel.

Balcony: Facing the Star Lake, the air is very fresh, the bathing pool is also very large, and the switch is electric. Compared with the traditional manual knob, this design is very smart and convenient. It is equipped with two sofa chairs, which makes the leisure feeling full.

Restaurant: On the first floor facing the Star Lake, you can take a walk by the lake after eating. There are many varieties of breakfast, which are also fresh and hygienic. The location is very spacious.

The only shortcoming is that the balcony is separated by a screen window, which should be considered for safety issues, especially for families with children staying together.

The overall feeling is very good and the decoration is also very new. It is suitable for business travel or family travel. I will come again in the future.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Garden-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted July 18, 2023
msg:It was the first time I stayed at Wyndham Hotel Qixingyan. I booked the unlimited outdoor mineral spring package for two mornings and two nights. The advantage is that the transportation is convenient, the hotel is very new, the room is large, clean and tidy. The hotel has a heated swimming pool, a fitness room, and an outdoor mineral spring that is very suitable for children. Unfortunately, the surf pool is not open on Sundays. The surrounding environment is also very good. There are lakes and greenways, and the scenery is good. Unfortunately, the typhoon this time has bad weather, and it will rain heavily at any time. I dare not rent electric cars and four-person bicycles. The disadvantage is that there are relatively few dishes for breakfast and dinner, and the replenishment is not timely enough. There are only 3 pots of fruit, and the leftover pot of water is not replaced after picking. Food quality is not good among hotels of the same level and needs to be improved. Finally, I would like to praise filex and Anna, the supervisor. The service attitude is very good, they are enthusiastic and take the initiative to answer questions, and the butler service is very considerate!
